add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #The Annexation of Flanders-Wallonia
	id = annex.1
	title = annex.1.t
	desc = annex.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		tag = FRA
		BEL = {
			has_capitulated = yes
		}
		controls_state = 6

	}
	option = {
		name = annex.1.a
		add_political_power = 60
		annex_country = {
			target = BEL
			transfer_troops = no
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	title = annex.2.t
	desc = annex.2.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = SWI
			tag = GER
		}
		controls_state = 3
		SWI = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SWITZ_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		if = {

			limit = {

				tag = FRA

			}

			SWI = {
				remove_state_core = 760
			}

		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {

				is_core_of = SWI
				is_controlled_by = ROOT

				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = SWI

		SWI = {
			add_state_core = 760
		}

		add_political_power = 100

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}


		set_country_flag = SWITZ_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}


country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	title = annex.3.t
	desc = annex.3.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = BUL has_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		}
		controls_state = 48
		BUL = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SER
			has_war_with = YUG
			has_war_with = TUR
			has_war_with = OTT
			has_war_with = ROM
			has_war_with = RRM
			has_war_with = GRE
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}
			BUL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BUL
		add_political_power = 100

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}



country_event = { #Romanian liberation
	id = annex.6
	title = annex.6.t
	desc = annex.6.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = ROM
			tag = RRM
		}
		controls_state = 46
		ROM = {
			exists = no
		}
		RRM = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ROM_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 82 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 82 }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 83 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 83 }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 76 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 76 }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 80 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 80 }
		}
		
		ROM = { add_state_core = 82
		add_state_core = 83
		add_state_core = 76
		add_state_core = 80
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROM
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}
			ROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			add_core_of = ROM
		}
		puppet = ROM
		add_political_power = 100

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUL
			}
			transfer_state = 772
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Take Bessarabia
		name = annex.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		trigger = { tag = RUS controls_state = 192 }
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 82 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 82 }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 83 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 83 }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 76 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 76 }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 80 }
		ROM = { add_state_core = 80 }
		}
		
		ROM = { add_state_core = 82
		add_state_core = 83
		add_state_core = 76
		add_state_core = 80
		}
		
		ROM = { remove_state_core = 78 }

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROM
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}
			ROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			add_core_of = ROM
		}
		puppet = ROM
		add_political_power = 100
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = ROM_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}



country_event = { #Serbian liberation
	id = annex.8
	title = annex.8.t
	desc = annex.8.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = SER
		}
		controls_state = 107
		OR = { NOT = { controls_state = 109 controls_state = 102 }
		AND = { OR = { controls_state = 109 controls_state = 102 } tag = AUS }
		}
		SER = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		}
		NOT = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = AHE
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SER
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}
			SER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SER
		add_political_power = 100

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}


country_event = { #greek liberation
	id = annex.10
	title = annex.10.t
	desc = annex.10.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = GRE
		}
		controls_state = 47
		GRE = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GRE_CONQ
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SER
			has_war_with = YUG
			has_war_with = TUR
			has_war_with = OTT
			has_war_with = ROM
			has_war_with = RRM
			has_war_with = ALB
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GRE
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					has_state_flag = bulgarian_macedonia #Ensures Central Macedonia is not transferred from Bulgaria to Greece
				}

			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = GRE
		add_political_power = 100

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = GRE_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}



country_event = { #HUN liberation
	id = annex.12
	title = annex.12.t
	desc = annex.12.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = HUN
			tag = AUS
			tag = AHE
			tag = DNF
		}
		controls_state = 43
		controls_state = 154
		controls_state = 155
		HUN = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_CONQ
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = AUS
			has_war_with = AHE
			has_war_with = DNF
			has_war_with = POL
			has_war_with = CRO
			has_war_with = BOS
			has_war_with = ILL
			has_war_with = GAL
			has_war_with = PLC
			has_war_with = BOM
			has_war_with = YUG
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate greater
		name = annex.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		
		if = { limit = { controls_state = 4 }
		remove_state_core = 784 }
		
		if = { limit = { OR = { controls_state = 4 AUS = { is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
		remove_state_core = 784 }

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HUN
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}
			HUN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = HUN
		add_political_power = 100

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}

	option = { #national hungary
		name = annex.12.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 94
		}
		HUN = {
			remove_state_core = 70
			remove_state_core = 71
			remove_state_core = 875
			remove_state_core = 82
			remove_state_core = 83
			remove_state_core = 76
			remove_state_core = 84
			remove_state_core = 789
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { controls_state = 91 GAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
		HUN = { remove_state_core = 73 }
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { controls_state = 4 AUS = { is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
		remove_state_core = 784 }
		set_country_flag = liberated_national_hungary
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HUN
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			}
			HUN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = HUN
		add_political_power = 100

	}
}


country_event = { #AUS liberation
	id = annex.14
	title = annex.14.t
	desc = annex.14.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = AUS
			tag = AHE
			tag = DNF
		}
		controls_state = 4
		AUS = {
			exists = no
		}
		AHE = {
			exists = no
		}
		DNF = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_CONQ
		}
		NOT = {
			4 = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {

				OR = {

					is_core_of = AUS

				}

			}

			AUS = {
				remove_state_core = PREV
			}

		}

		AUS = {

			add_state_core = 153
			add_state_core = 836
			add_state_core = 775
			add_state_core = 4
			add_state_core = 152
			add_state_core = 835
			add_state_core = 39
			add_state_core = 784

		}


		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AUS
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}


			}

			AUS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ITA
					tag = SRI
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 783
			transfer_state = 39
			transfer_state = 759
			transfer_state = 736
			transfer_state = 795
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = { is_subject_of = ROOT controls_state = 784 }
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = 784 }
		}
		puppet = AUS
		add_political_power = 100

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}

	option = { #old idea
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = EMP
			tag = REB
			}
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = GRU
			}
		}
		name = annex.14.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 79
		}
		country_event = {
			id = annex.15
		}
	}
}

		add_state_core = 835
		add_state_core = 784
		add_state_core = 39
		add_state_core = 783
		add_state_core = 736

country_event = { #Austrian Italy liberation
	id = annex.17
	title = annex.17.t
	desc = annex.17.d
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = AUS
			tag = AHE
			tag = DNF
			tag = ITA
			tag = SRI
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = ITA
			has_war_with = SRI
		}
		controls_state = 759
		NOT = { controls_state = 2 }
		NOT = { controls_state = 4 }
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NTA_CONQ
		}
		NOT = {
			759 = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #Give Italy
		name = annex.17.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = EMP
			tag = REB
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = ITA
				is_in_faction_with = SRI
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ITA
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = annex.18
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SRI
			}
			SRI = {
				country_event = {
					id = annex.18
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = NTA_CONQ
		add_political_power = -20
	}

	option = { #Puppet them
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = EMP
			tag = REB
			}
			ITA = {
				exists = no
			}
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialist has_government = syndicalist has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		name = annex.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 9
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 783
			transfer_state = 39
			transfer_state = 759
			transfer_state = 736
			transfer_state = 795
			add_state_core = 783
			add_state_core = 39
			add_state_core = 759
			add_state_core = 736
			add_state_core = 795
		}
		puppet = ITA

	}
	
	option = { #Give Austria
		name = annex.17.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				AUS = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		AUS = {
		transfer_state = 783
		transfer_state = 759
		transfer_state = 736
		transfer_state = 795
		add_state_core = 783
		add_state_core = 759
		add_state_core = 736
		add_state_core = 795
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Give Austria and give istria to slovenia
		name = annex.17.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
			}
			AND = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				AUS = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = SLO
				SLO = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		AUS = {
		transfer_state = 783
		transfer_state = 759
		transfer_state = 795
		add_state_core = 783
		add_state_core = 759
		add_state_core = 795
		}
		SLO = {
		transfer_state = 736
		add_state_core = 736
		}
	}
}

	id = annex.21

	trigger = {

		}

			tag = SLO
			tag = AUS
			tag = DNF
			tag = AHE
			tag = ILL
		}
		controls_state = 102
		NOT = { AND = { controls_state = 109 controls_state = 107 } 
		102 = { is_core_of = ROOT }
		}
		SLO = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SLO_CONQ
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SER
			has_war_with = YUG

	id = annex.45
	title = annex.45.t
	desc = annex.45.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.45.a
		clr_country_flag = ITA_deal_ongoing
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = AHE
				}
			}
			SRI = {
				remove_state_core = 783
				remove_state_core = 39
				remove_state_core = 759
				remove_state_core = 795
				remove_state_core = 736
			}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SRI
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			create_faction = "Alliance"
			add_to_faction = ITA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					is_in_faction = yes is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			add_to_faction = ITA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					is_in_faction = yes NOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				add_to_faction = ITA
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		controls_state = 761

		}

	}

			factor = 35
		}

		add_state_claim = 761

			remove_state_core = 151

		}

					is_core_of = ROOT

			}

				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = SWI

		SWI = {

			add_state_core = 151

		}

		}
		country_event = {
			id = annex.91
		}
	}

						}

						}

					}

						exists = yes

							controls_state = 735

							controls_state = 159

					}

					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ITA
					}

				}

			}

		}

		name = annex.89.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}

		add_state_claim = 761

			id = annex.90 days = 360
		}

			limit = {
				FRP = {
					exists = yes controls_state = 17
				}
			}

				country_event = {

				}
			}

				}
			}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = PREV

				is_core_of = GBR

			}
			GBR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}
		puppet = GBR
		GBR = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GBR_republic
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy all
		name = annex.132.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Brazil
	id = annex.181
	title = annex.181.t
	desc = annex.181.d

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			tag = EMP
			tag = REB
		}

		NOT = {
			original_tag = BRA
			tag = PIR
			has_war_with = PIR
			has_war_with = ARG
			has_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
			country_exists = BRA
		}

		controls_state = 500
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = { #liberate full brazil
		name = annex.181.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = BRA
		
		if = { limit = { tag = ARG BRA = { controls_state = 504 } }
		transfer_state = 504
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Liberate Piratini
		name = annex.181.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = { factor = 0
			NOT = { tag = ARG is_ai = no }
			}
		}
		
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PIR
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			PIR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = PIR

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = BRA
		
		if = { limit = { tag = ARG BRA = { controls_state = 504 } }
		transfer_state = 504
		}
		
		if = { limit = { tag = ARG }
		set_country_flag = ARG_beat_bra
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		set_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
	}
}
